TITLE: Medical Device Sales Representative
CATEGORY: Sales & Business Development
AVG SALARY: $155,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
We are seeking a driven, clinically credible Medical Device Sales Representative to own a defined territory and grow market share for our device portfolio. This is a field-based role requiring exceptional relationship-building skills, surgical environment comfort, and the commercial instincts to convert competitive accounts. You will be the face of {{company_name}} to surgeons, OR directors, and hospital administration.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Manage and grow an assigned territory by calling on hospitals, ASCs, physician offices, and IDNs to promote and sell the company's device portfolio
• Attend and provide in-room clinical support during surgical procedures, ensuring optimal device utilization and physician confidence
• Build and maintain executive-level relationships with OR directors, materials management, and key surgeons
• Meet or exceed quarterly and annual revenue quotas while maintaining accurate pipeline forecasting in CRM
• Conduct product demonstrations, in-services, and trials to drive new account conversions and competitive displacements
• Collaborate with clinical specialists and marketing on territory launch plans and promotional activities
• Respond to competitive threats with compelling clinical and economic value messaging
• Maintain compliance with all healthcare industry regulations including Sunshine Act reporting and hospital credentialing requirements

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 2+ years of medical device, pharmaceutical, or healthcare sales experience
• Documented history of meeting or exceeding sales quota
• Ability to work flexible hours including early mornings for OR cases
• Valid driver's license and ability to travel 60–80% within territory
• Strong clinical acumen and comfort in surgical environments
• Bachelor's degree required (Life Sciences, Business, or related field preferred)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Experience with implantables, capital equipment, or surgical disposables
• Existing relationships with orthopedic, cardiovascular, or surgical accounts
• Familiarity with hospital GPO/IDN contracting processes
• CRM proficiency (Salesforce or equivalent)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Top performers earn $200K+ total compensation with uncapped commission
• Sell a clinically differentiated product with strong outcomes data

• Work with world-class surgeons and make a daily impact on patient outcomes

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $130,000–$175,000 base
• Target Bonus: Up to 30% of base
• Equity: Typically none at this level
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — quota attainment, territory background, and motivations
2. Hiring manager video call (60 min) — sales process, clinical acumen, competitive wins
3. Field ride-along or virtual business review — demonstrate territory planning and account strategy
4. Panel interview with sales leadership and marketing — cross-functional fit
5. Reference checks and offer

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your best competitive displacement — what was the account, the obstacle, and how you won it.
Q2: What does your prospecting process look like for a cold OR account you've never been in?
Q3: Describe a time you lost a key account and what you did to recover it.
Q4: How do you manage a territory where you're in the OR at 6am and also need to make afternoon office calls?
Q5: What is your current quota and where are you tracking YTD?
Q6: How do you build a relationship with an OR director who doesn't want reps in their department?
Q7: Tell me about the most complex capital equipment sale you've closed and what made it difficult.
Q8: How do you stay current on clinical literature relevant to your product line?
Q9: Walk me through your CRM pipeline management process.
Q10: What's your approach to converting a surgeon who has used a competitor product for 10+ years?

POSITION OVERVIEW

The Territory Sales Manager owns all commercial activity within an assigned geography, managing a diverse account base from large IDNs to independent physician practices. This is a high-accountability role for a self-directed sales professional who thrives in a competitive market and can execute both strategic account development and day-to-day sales activity.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Own revenue performance across a defined geographic territory for the full device portfolio
• Develop and execute territory business plans with 90-day, 6-month, and annual milestones
• Prospect new accounts while protecting and growing existing customer relationships
• Manage distributor or rep agency relationships where applicable
• Coordinate clinical, technical, and marketing resources to support territory initiatives
• Provide accurate monthly and quarterly revenue forecasts to sales leadership
• Represent the company at regional trade shows, symposia, and professional society meetings
• Ensure all activity complies with AdvaMed Code of Ethics and company compliance policies

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• 3+ years of territory-based medical device sales experience
• Consistent quota attainment at 100%+ over the last two years
• Experience managing complex, multi-stakeholder sales cycles
• Strong analytical skills for territory planning and forecasting
• Bachelor's degree required

TITLE: Senior Sales Representative
CATEGORY: Sales & Business Development
AVG SALARY: $165,000

ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
The Senior Sales Representative is the highest individual contributor sales role, responsible for {{company_name}}'s most strategically important accounts. This individual brings deep clinical expertise, executive-level relationship skills, and a track record of closing complex, multi-stakeholder deals in a competitive device market.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Manage a portfolio of high-value accounts including large hospital systems, academic medical centers, and complex surgical programs
• Act as primary commercial contact for surgeons and hospital administration at named strategic accounts
• Mentor and support junior territory reps through ride-alongs, case support, and business planning
• Lead capital equipment evaluation processes from clinical trial through committee approval and contract execution
• Present clinical outcomes data, health economic analyses, and competitive comparisons to key stakeholders
• Develop account-level strategic plans with quarterly milestones reviewed with regional management
• Support new product launches by seeding target accounts and generating early clinical adoption
• Contribute to regional sales strategy meetings and serve as a subject matter resource to peers

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 5+ years of medical device sales with consistent top-quartile performance
• Experience selling to complex, multi-stakeholder hospital accounts
• Strong clinical comfort level — able to speak fluently to surgeons about anatomy, technique, and device performance
• Track record of closing capital equipment and implantable contracts
• Bachelor's degree required

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in implantable devices, robotics, or capital equipment
• Clinical or scientific background (nursing, biology, kinesiology) preferred
• Formal sales training certification (SPIN, Challenger, etc.)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Highest-earning individual contributor role in the commercial organization

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Q6: Tell me about a deal that took over 12 months to close. What made it difficult?
Q7: How do you differentiate yourself from a competitor rep who has been in the account longer than you?
Q8: Describe how you use clinical data in a sales conversation without overwhelming the customer.
Q9: What is your biggest account and what is your plan for it in the next 12 months?
Q10: How do you stay organized when managing 50+ active accounts across a large geography?

TITLE: Regional Sales Manager
CATEGORY: Sales & Business Development
AVG SALARY: $170,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
The Regional Sales Manager leads a field team of territory representatives across a multi-state region, accountable for regional revenue, team development, and strategic market execution. This is a people-first leadership role that demands both commercial acumen and the ability to coach, inspire, and hold a team accountable to results.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Lead a team of 6–12 territory sales representatives across a defined multi-state region
• Set and communicate quarterly and annual revenue targets by territory aligned to national plan
• Coach reps through field visits, ride-alongs, and regular 1:1 development sessions
• Own regional revenue forecast accuracy and report pipeline status to VP/Director of Sales weekly
• Recruit, hire, onboard, and develop high-performing territory reps
• Partner with clinical affairs, marketing, and operations teams to execute regional programs
• Manage key strategic accounts at the regional level and support reps in major opportunity pursuits
• Build and maintain relationships with regional KOLs, hospital system executives, and GPO representatives

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• 5+ years of medical device field sales experience with 2+ years in a management or team lead capacity
• Track record of building and developing high-performing sales teams
• Strong financial acumen — able to read and manage P&L, forecast revenue, and analyze territory performance
• Experience recruiting and onboarding sales talent
• Bachelor's degree required; MBA a plus

Q1: Tell me about the largest team you have managed. How many reps and what was the geographic scope?
Q2: Walk me through how you coach a rep who is technically strong but struggles to close.
Q3: Describe a time you had to terminate a rep for performance. How did you handle it?

Q5: How do you prioritize your time across a large, geographically dispersed team?
Q6: Tell me about a time you had to turn around a low-performing territory quickly.
Q7: How do you build a recruiting pipeline so you are never more than 30 days away from a strong candidate?
Q8: Describe your forecast cadence. How accurate are you and what do you do when a deal slips?
Q9: How do you balance spending time with top performers vs. struggling reps?
Q10: What is your management philosophy and how has it evolved?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing VP of Sales to join our Sales & Business Development team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Develop and execute territory or account-level sales plans aligned to annual revenue targets
• Build and maintain strategic relationships with clinical, administrative, and procurement decision-makers
• Conduct product demonstrations, in-services, and procedure support for device adoption
• Manage competitive displacement opportunities through differentiated value messaging
• Maintain accurate pipeline data and provide reliable revenue forecasts in CRM
• Coordinate with clinical, marketing, and operations resources to support customer needs
• Ensure full compliance with AdvaMed guidelines, hospital credentialing, and Sunshine Act reporting

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 2+ years of medical device or healthcare sales experience
• Consistent track record of quota attainment
• Comfort in clinical environments including operating rooms, cath labs, or ICUs
• Valid driver's license; ability to travel within assigned territory
• Bachelor's degree required

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Existing relationships with target customer segment (surgeons, IDNs, hospital systems)
• CRM proficiency (Salesforce preferred)
• Clinical or scientific background a plus

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Sales & Business Development professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $200,000–$280,000 base
• Target Bonus: 50–100% of base
• Equity: Significant equity package
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this VP of Sales role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $110,000–$150,000 base
• Target Bonus: 15–25% of base
• Equity: Equity at some companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Business Development Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Account Executive
CATEGORY: Sales & Business Development
AVG SALARY: $120,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Account Executive to join our Sales & Business Development team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Develop and execute territory or account-level sales plans aligned to annual revenue targets
• Build and maintain strategic relationships with clinical, administrative, and procurement decision-makers
• Conduct product demonstrations, in-services, and procedure support for device adoption
• Manage competitive displacement opportunities through differentiated value messaging
• Maintain accurate pipeline data and provide reliable revenue forecasts in CRM
• Coordinate with clinical, marketing, and operations resources to support customer needs
• Ensure full compliance with AdvaMed guidelines, hospital credentialing, and Sunshine Act reporting

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 2+ years of medical device or healthcare sales experience
• Consistent track record of quota attainment
• Comfort in clinical environments including operating rooms, cath labs, or ICUs
• Valid driver's license; ability to travel within assigned territory
• Bachelor's degree required

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Existing relationships with target customer segment (surgeons, IDNs, hospital systems)
• CRM proficiency (Salesforce preferred)
• Clinical or scientific background a plus

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Sales & Business Development professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $95,000–$140,000 base
• Target Bonus: 20–30% of base
• Equity: None typically
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Develop and execute territory or account-level sales plans aligned to annual revenue targets
• Build and maintain strategic relationships with clinical, administrative, and procurement decision-makers
• Conduct product demonstrations, in-services, and procedure support for device adoption
• Manage competitive displacement opportunities through differentiated value messaging
• Maintain accurate pipeline data and provide reliable revenue forecasts in CRM
• Coordinate with clinical, marketing, and operations resources to support customer needs
• Ensure full compliance with AdvaMed guidelines, hospital credentialing, and Sunshine Act reporting

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 2+ years of medical device or healthcare sales experience
• Consistent track record of quota attainment
• Comfort in clinical environments including operating rooms, cath labs, or ICUs
• Valid driver's license; ability to travel within assigned territory
• Bachelor's degree required

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Existing relationships with target customer segment (surgeons, IDNs, hospital systems)
• CRM proficiency (Salesforce preferred)
• Clinical or scientific background a plus

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Sales & Business Development professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $120,000–$165,000 base
• Target Bonus: 20–30% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Key Account Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Orthopedic Sales Representative role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

CATEGORY: Sales & Business Development
AVG SALARY: $175,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Cardiovascular Sales Specialist to join our Sales & Business Development team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Develop and execute territory or account-level sales plans aligned to annual revenue targets
• Build and maintain strategic relationships with clinical, administrative, and procurement decision-makers
• Conduct product demonstrations, in-services, and procedure support for device adoption
• Manage competitive displacement opportunities through differentiated value messaging
• Maintain accurate pipeline data and provide reliable revenue forecasts in CRM
• Coordinate with clinical, marketing, and operations resources to support customer needs
• Ensure full compliance with AdvaMed guidelines, hospital credentialing, and Sunshine Act reporting

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• 2+ years of medical device or healthcare sales experience
• Consistent track record of quota attainment
• Comfort in clinical environments including operating rooms, cath labs, or ICUs
• Valid driver's license; ability to travel within assigned territory
• Bachelor's degree required

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Train and educate clinical staff, physicians, and hospital personnel on safe and effective device use
• Develop clinical training materials, protocols, and educational content for internal and external use
• Serve as the primary clinical resource for key accounts, KOLs, and investigational sites
• Collect and communicate clinical feedback to R&D, marketing, and regulatory teams
• Support regulatory submissions with clinical data, study protocols, and post-market evidence
• Manage relationships with clinical investigators, IRBs, and study coordinators where applicable

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Clinical background in nursing, cardiovascular technology, clinical research, or related field — OR equivalent experience in medical device clinical support
• Hands-on experience in a procedural clinical environment (OR, cath lab, EP lab, or equivalent)
• Strong communication skills for translating technical concepts to clinical audiences
• Ability to travel 40–60% within assigned region

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Advanced clinical certification (RN, RCIS, RCES, CCT) or graduate degree in clinical/life sciences
• Experience with clinical trial management or post-market surveillance activities
• GCP certification

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Clinical & Applications professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $95,000–$130,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: None typically
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Clinical Specialist role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

CATEGORY: Clinical & Applications
AVG SALARY: $120,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Clinical Applications Manager to join our Clinical & Applications team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Clinical Affairs Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Clinical Research Associate (CRA)
CATEGORY: Clinical & Applications
AVG SALARY: $90,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Clinical Research Associate (CRA) to join our Clinical & Applications team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Provide clinical support and product expertise to healthcare professionals in procedural environments
• Train and educate clinical staff, physicians, and hospital personnel on safe and effective device use
• Develop clinical training materials, protocols, and educational content for internal and external use
• Serve as the primary clinical resource for key accounts, KOLs, and investigational sites
• Collect and communicate clinical feedback to R&D, marketing, and regulatory teams
• Support regulatory submissions with clinical data, study protocols, and post-market evidence
• Manage relationships with clinical investigators, IRBs, and study coordinators where applicable

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Clinical background in nursing, cardiovascular technology, clinical research, or related field — OR equivalent experience in medical device clinical support
• Hands-on experience in a procedural clinical environment (OR, cath lab, EP lab, or equivalent)
• Strong communication skills for translating technical concepts to clinical audiences
• Ability to travel 40–60% within assigned region

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Advanced clinical certification (RN, RCIS, RCES, CCT) or graduate degree in clinical/life sciences
• Experience with clinical trial management or post-market surveillance activities
• GCP certification

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Clinical & Applications professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $75,000–$105,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: None
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Clinical background in nursing, cardiovascular technology, clinical research, or related field — OR equivalent experience in medical device clinical support
• Hands-on experience in a procedural clinical environment (OR, cath lab, EP lab, or equivalent)
• Strong communication skills for translating technical concepts to clinical audiences
• Ability to travel 40–60% within assigned region

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Advanced clinical certification (RN, RCIS, RCES, CCT) or graduate degree in clinical/life sciences
• Experience with clinical trial management or post-market surveillance activities
• GCP certification

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Clinical & Applications professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $88,000–$122,000 base
• Target Bonus: 8–12% of base
• Equity: None typically
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Clinical Data Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Principal Clinical Scientist
CATEGORY: Clinical & Applications
AVG SALARY: $145,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Principal Clinical Scientist to join our Clinical & Applications team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Provide clinical support and product expertise to healthcare professionals in procedural environments
• Train and educate clinical staff, physicians, and hospital personnel on safe and effective device use
• Develop clinical training materials, protocols, and educational content for internal and external use
• Serve as the primary clinical resource for key accounts, KOLs, and investigational sites
• Collect and communicate clinical feedback to R&D, marketing, and regulatory teams
• Support regulatory submissions with clinical data, study protocols, and post-market evidence
• Manage relationships with clinical investigators, IRBs, and study coordinators where applicable

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Clinical background in nursing, cardiovascular technology, clinical research, or related field — OR equivalent experience in medical device clinical support
• Hands-on experience in a procedural clinical environment (OR, cath lab, EP lab, or equivalent)
• Strong communication skills for translating technical concepts to clinical audiences
• Ability to travel 40–60% within assigned region

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?

TITLE: Medical Science Liaison (MSL)
CATEGORY: Clinical & Applications
AVG SALARY: $160,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Medical Science Liaison (MSL) to join our Clinical & Applications team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Provide clinical support and product expertise to healthcare professionals in procedural environments
• Train and educate clinical staff, physicians, and hospital personnel on safe and effective device use
• Develop clinical training materials, protocols, and educational content for internal and external use
• Serve as the primary clinical resource for key accounts, KOLs, and investigational sites
• Collect and communicate clinical feedback to R&D, marketing, and regulatory teams
• Support regulatory submissions with clinical data, study protocols, and post-market evidence
• Manage relationships with clinical investigators, IRBs, and study coordinators where applicable

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Clinical background in nursing, cardiovascular technology, clinical research, or related field — OR equivalent experience in medical device clinical support
• Hands-on experience in a procedural clinical environment (OR, cath lab, EP lab, or equivalent)
• Strong communication skills for translating technical concepts to clinical audiences
• Ability to travel 40–60% within assigned region

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Advanced clinical certification (RN, RCIS, RCES, CCT) or graduate degree in clinical/life sciences
• Experience with clinical trial management or post-market surveillance activities
• GCP certification

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Clinical & Applications professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $135,000–$185,000 base
• Target Bonus: 10–15% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

TITLE: Field Service Engineer
CATEGORY: Field Service & Technical Support
AVG SALARY: $80,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Field Service Engineer to join our Field Service & Technical Support team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Install, maintain, troubleshoot, and repair medical device systems at customer sites
• Perform scheduled and unscheduled preventive maintenance per established service protocols
• Document all service activities in CRM and complaint management systems accurately and on time
• Train customers on proper equipment operation, cleaning, and basic troubleshooting
• Escalate unresolved technical issues to engineering with complete documentation of findings
• Manage parts inventory and logistics to minimize equipment downtime at customer sites
• Maintain all required hospital credentialing, vaccination records, and compliance certifications

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Technical degree or equivalent experience in electronics, biomedical engineering, or related field
• Hands-on mechanical and electrical troubleshooting experience
• Ability to travel 50–80% within assigned service territory
• Strong customer-facing communication skills and professional presence
• Valid driver's license

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BMET certification or equivalent
• Experience with capital medical equipment (imaging, infusion, diagnostic, or surgical systems)
• Familiarity with FDA complaint handling and MDR reporting requirements

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Field Service & Technical Support professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Target Bonus: 5–8% of base
• Equity: None
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Field Service Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Senior Field Service Engineer
CATEGORY: Field Service & Technical Support
AVG SALARY: $97,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Senior Field Service Engineer to join our Field Service & Technical Support team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Install, maintain, troubleshoot, and repair medical device systems at customer sites
• Perform scheduled and unscheduled preventive maintenance per established service protocols
• Document all service activities in CRM and complaint management systems accurately and on time
• Train customers on proper equipment operation, cleaning, and basic troubleshooting
• Escalate unresolved technical issues to engineering with complete documentation of findings
• Manage parts inventory and logistics to minimize equipment downtime at customer sites
• Maintain all required hospital credentialing, vaccination records, and compliance certifications

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Applications Engineer
CATEGORY: Field Service & Technical Support
AVG SALARY: $95,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Applications Engineer to join our Field Service & Technical Support team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Install, maintain, troubleshoot, and repair medical device systems at customer sites
• Perform scheduled and unscheduled preventive maintenance per established service protocols
• Document all service activities in CRM and complaint management systems accurately and on time
• Train customers on proper equipment operation, cleaning, and basic troubleshooting
• Escalate unresolved technical issues to engineering with complete documentation of findings
• Manage parts inventory and logistics to minimize equipment downtime at customer sites
• Maintain all required hospital credentialing, vaccination records, and compliance certifications

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Technical degree or equivalent experience in electronics, biomedical engineering, or related field
• Hands-on mechanical and electrical troubleshooting experience
• Ability to travel 50–80% within assigned service territory
• Strong customer-facing communication skills and professional presence
• Valid driver's license

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BMET certification or equivalent
• Experience with capital medical equipment (imaging, infusion, diagnostic, or surgical systems)
• Familiarity with FDA complaint handling and MDR reporting requirements

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Field Service & Technical Support professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

• Install, maintain, troubleshoot, and repair medical device systems at customer sites
• Perform scheduled and unscheduled preventive maintenance per established service protocols
• Document all service activities in CRM and complaint management systems accurately and on time
• Train customers on proper equipment operation, cleaning, and basic troubleshooting
• Escalate unresolved technical issues to engineering with complete documentation of findings
• Manage parts inventory and logistics to minimize equipment downtime at customer sites
• Maintain all required hospital credentialing, vaccination records, and compliance certifications

• Technical degree or equivalent experience in electronics, biomedical engineering, or related field
• Hands-on mechanical and electrical troubleshooting experience
• Ability to travel 50–80% within assigned service territory
• Strong customer-facing communication skills and professional presence
• Valid driver's license

TITLE: R&D Engineer
CATEGORY: Engineering – R&D & Design
AVG SALARY: $100,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing R&D Engineer to join our Engineering – R&D & Design team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, develop, and test medical device components and systems following design control procedures (21 CFR 820.30, ISO 13485)
• Author and execute design verification and validation (V&V) test protocols and reports
• Maintain design history file (DHF) documentation including design inputs, outputs, risk analyses, and traceability matrices
• Conduct failure analysis on design-related issues using FMEA, fault tree analysis, and root cause investigation methods
• Collaborate with manufacturing, quality, and regulatory teams during design transfer and new product introduction
• Apply engineering first principles to solve complex design challenges and improve product performance
• Identify, evaluate, and qualify materials, components, and processes for regulatory and performance compliance

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BS in Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Biomedical Engineering, or related discipline
• Experience with medical device design under FDA QSR or ISO 13485
• Proficiency with CAD tools (SolidWorks, CATIA) or relevant engineering software
• Understanding of design controls, risk management (ISO 14971), and V&V methodology

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• MS or PhD in engineering or related field
• Experience with design transfer and NPI processes

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Design Engineer to join our Engineering – R&D & Design team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, develop, and test medical device components and systems following design control procedures (21 CFR 820.30, ISO 13485)
• Author and execute design verification and validation (V&V) test protocols and reports
• Maintain design history file (DHF) documentation including design inputs, outputs, risk analyses, and traceability matrices
• Conduct failure analysis on design-related issues using FMEA, fault tree analysis, and root cause investigation methods
• Collaborate with manufacturing, quality, and regulatory teams during design transfer and new product introduction
• Apply engineering first principles to solve complex design challenges and improve product performance
• Identify, evaluate, and qualify materials, components, and processes for regulatory and performance compliance

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BS in Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Biomedical Engineering, or related discipline
• Experience with medical device design under FDA QSR or ISO 13485
• Proficiency with CAD tools (SolidWorks, CATIA) or relevant engineering software
• Understanding of design controls, risk management (ISO 14971), and V&V methodology

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• MS or PhD in engineering or related field
• Experience with design transfer and NPI processes
• Familiarity with ISO 10993 biocompatibility or IEC 60601 electrical safety standards
• Patent filings or publications in relevant technical domains

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Engineering – R&D & Design professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $84,000–$112,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Design Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Engineering – R&D & Design professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

INTERVIEW PROCESS

1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Electrical Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Software Engineer
CATEGORY: Engineering – R&D & Design
AVG SALARY: $115,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Software Engineer to join our Engineering – R&D & Design team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, develop, and test medical device components and systems following design control procedures (21 CFR 820.30, ISO 13485)
• Author and execute design verification and validation (V&V) test protocols and reports
• Maintain design history file (DHF) documentation including design inputs, outputs, risk analyses, and traceability matrices
• Conduct failure analysis on design-related issues using FMEA, fault tree analysis, and root cause investigation methods
• Collaborate with manufacturing, quality, and regulatory teams during design transfer and new product introduction
• Apply engineering first principles to solve complex design challenges and improve product performance
• Identify, evaluate, and qualify materials, components, and processes for regulatory and performance compliance

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BS in Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Biomedical Engineering, or related discipline
• Experience with medical device design under FDA QSR or ISO 13485
• Proficiency with CAD tools (SolidWorks, CATIA) or relevant engineering software
• Understanding of design controls, risk management (ISO 14971), and V&V methodology

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• MS or PhD in engineering or related field
• Experience with design transfer and NPI processes
• Familiarity with ISO 10993 biocompatibility or IEC 60601 electrical safety standards
• Patent filings or publications in relevant technical domains
