━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Product Development Engineer to join our Engineering – R&D & Design team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, develop, and test medical device components and systems following design control procedures (21 CFR 820.30, ISO 13485)
• Author and execute design verification and validation (V&V) test protocols and reports
• Maintain design history file (DHF) documentation including design inputs, outputs, risk analyses, and traceability matrices
• Conduct failure analysis on design-related issues using FMEA, fault tree analysis, and root cause investigation methods
• Collaborate with manufacturing, quality, and regulatory teams during design transfer and new product introduction
• Apply engineering first principles to solve complex design challenges and improve product performance
• Identify, evaluate, and qualify materials, components, and processes for regulatory and performance compliance

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BS in Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Biomedical Engineering, or related discipline
• Experience with medical device design under FDA QSR or ISO 13485
• Proficiency with CAD tools (SolidWorks, CATIA) or relevant engineering software
• Understanding of design controls, risk management (ISO 14971), and V&V methodology

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• MS or PhD in engineering or related field
• Experience with design transfer and NPI processes
• Familiarity with ISO 10993 biocompatibility or IEC 60601 electrical safety standards
• Patent filings or publications in relevant technical domains

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Engineering – R&D & Design professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $89,000–$118,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Product Development Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Senior R&D Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Principal Engineer
CATEGORY: Engineering – R&D & Design
AVG SALARY: $150,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Principal Engineer to join our Engineering – R&D & Design team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, develop, and test medical device components and systems following design control procedures (21 CFR 820.30, ISO 13485)
• Author and execute design verification and validation (V&V) test protocols and reports
• Maintain design history file (DHF) documentation including design inputs, outputs, risk analyses, and traceability matrices
• Conduct failure analysis on design-related issues using FMEA, fault tree analysis, and root cause investigation methods
• Collaborate with manufacturing, quality, and regulatory teams during design transfer and new product introduction
• Apply engineering first principles to solve complex design challenges and improve product performance
• Identify, evaluate, and qualify materials, components, and processes for regulatory and performance compliance

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BS in Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Biomedical Engineering, or related discipline
• Experience with medical device design under FDA QSR or ISO 13485
• Proficiency with CAD tools (SolidWorks, CATIA) or relevant engineering software
• Understanding of design controls, risk management (ISO 14971), and V&V methodology

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• MS or PhD in engineering or related field
• Experience with design transfer and NPI processes
• Familiarity with ISO 10993 biocompatibility or IEC 60601 electrical safety standards
• Patent filings or publications in relevant technical domains

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Packaging Engineer to join our Engineering – R&D & Design team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, develop, and test medical device components and systems following design control procedures (21 CFR 820.30, ISO 13485)
• Author and execute design verification and validation (V&V) test protocols and reports
• Maintain design history file (DHF) documentation including design inputs, outputs, risk analyses, and traceability matrices
• Conduct failure analysis on design-related issues using FMEA, fault tree analysis, and root cause investigation methods
• Collaborate with manufacturing, quality, and regulatory teams during design transfer and new product introduction
• Apply engineering first principles to solve complex design challenges and improve product performance
• Identify, evaluate, and qualify materials, components, and processes for regulatory and performance compliance

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• BS in Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Biomedical Engineering, or related discipline
• Experience with medical device design under FDA QSR or ISO 13485
• Proficiency with CAD tools (SolidWorks, CATIA) or relevant engineering software
• Understanding of design controls, risk management (ISO 14971), and V&V methodology

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• MS or PhD in engineering or related field
• Experience with design transfer and NPI processes
• Familiarity with ISO 10993 biocompatibility or IEC 60601 electrical safety standards
• Patent filings or publications in relevant technical domains

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Engineering – R&D & Design professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $76,000–$102,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–8% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Packaging Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Quality Engineer
CATEGORY: Quality & Regulatory
AVG SALARY: $90,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Quality Engineer to join our Quality & Regulatory team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Maintain and improve quality management system (QMS) processes in accordance with ISO 13485, 21 CFR Part 820, and applicable international standards
• Author, review, and approve quality documentation including SOPs, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate nonconformances, customer complaints, and CAPAs using structured root cause analysis methodologies (5-Why, fishbone, fault tree)
• Support regulatory submissions including 510(k)s, CE technical files, and post-market surveillance reports
• Lead or participate in internal, supplier, and regulatory agency audits
• Interface with FDA, notified bodies, and international regulatory authorities on compliance matters
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives to reduce defects, improve yield, and strengthen quality culture

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device environment under ISO 13485 or FDA QSR
• Working knowledge of CAPA, change control, and complaint handling processes
• Familiarity with design controls (21 CFR Part 820.30) and associated documentation
• Strong written communication skills for authoring technical documents and regulatory submissions
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Life Sciences, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• ASQ certification (CQE, CQA, or CQPA)
• Experience with MDD/MDR or IVDR regulatory frameworks
• Proficiency with electronic QMS platforms (Veeva Vault, Greenlight Guru, MasterControl)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?

Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Senior Quality Engineer
CATEGORY: Quality & Regulatory
AVG SALARY: $108,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Senior Quality Engineer to join our Quality & Regulatory team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Maintain and improve quality management system (QMS) processes in accordance with ISO 13485, 21 CFR Part 820, and applicable international standards
• Author, review, and approve quality documentation including SOPs, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate nonconformances, customer complaints, and CAPAs using structured root cause analysis methodologies (5-Why, fishbone, fault tree)
• Support regulatory submissions including 510(k)s, CE technical files, and post-market surveillance reports
• Lead or participate in internal, supplier, and regulatory agency audits
• Interface with FDA, notified bodies, and international regulatory authorities on compliance matters
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives to reduce defects, improve yield, and strengthen quality culture

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device environment under ISO 13485 or FDA QSR
• Working knowledge of CAPA, change control, and complaint handling processes
• Familiarity with design controls (21 CFR Part 820.30) and associated documentation
• Strong written communication skills for authoring technical documents and regulatory submissions
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Life Sciences, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Director of Quality Assurance to join our Quality & Regulatory team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Maintain and improve quality management system (QMS) processes in accordance with ISO 13485, 21 CFR Part 820, and applicable international standards
• Author, review, and approve quality documentation including SOPs, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate nonconformances, customer complaints, and CAPAs using structured root cause analysis methodologies (5-Why, fishbone, fault tree)
• Support regulatory submissions including 510(k)s, CE technical files, and post-market surveillance reports
• Lead or participate in internal, supplier, and regulatory agency audits
• Interface with FDA, notified bodies, and international regulatory authorities on compliance matters
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives to reduce defects, improve yield, and strengthen quality culture

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device environment under ISO 13485 or FDA QSR
• Working knowledge of CAPA, change control, and complaint handling processes
• Familiarity with design controls (21 CFR Part 820.30) and associated documentation
• Strong written communication skills for authoring technical documents and regulatory submissions
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Life Sciences, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• ASQ certification (CQE, CQA, or CQPA)
• Experience with MDD/MDR or IVDR regulatory frameworks
• Proficiency with electronic QMS platforms (Veeva Vault, Greenlight Guru, MasterControl)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Quality & Regulatory professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $143,000–$188,000 base
• Target Bonus: 15–25% of base
• Equity: Significant equity package
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Director of Quality Assurance role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

• Proficiency with electronic QMS platforms (Veeva Vault, Greenlight Guru, MasterControl)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

INTERVIEW PROCESS

1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Quality Control Inspector role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Quality Control Technician
CATEGORY: Quality & Regulatory
AVG SALARY: $55,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Quality Control Technician to join our Quality & Regulatory team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Maintain and improve quality management system (QMS) processes in accordance with ISO 13485, 21 CFR Part 820, and applicable international standards
• Author, review, and approve quality documentation including SOPs, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate nonconformances, customer complaints, and CAPAs using structured root cause analysis methodologies (5-Why, fishbone, fault tree)
• Support regulatory submissions including 510(k)s, CE technical files, and post-market surveillance reports
• Lead or participate in internal, supplier, and regulatory agency audits
• Interface with FDA, notified bodies, and international regulatory authorities on compliance matters
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives to reduce defects, improve yield, and strengthen quality culture

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device environment under ISO 13485 or FDA QSR
• Working knowledge of CAPA, change control, and complaint handling processes
• Familiarity with design controls (21 CFR Part 820.30) and associated documentation
• Strong written communication skills for authoring technical documents and regulatory submissions
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Life Sciences, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Verification & Validation Engineer to join our Quality & Regulatory team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Maintain and improve quality management system (QMS) processes in accordance with ISO 13485, 21 CFR Part 820, and applicable international standards
• Author, review, and approve quality documentation including SOPs, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate nonconformances, customer complaints, and CAPAs using structured root cause analysis methodologies (5-Why, fishbone, fault tree)
• Support regulatory submissions including 510(k)s, CE technical files, and post-market surveillance reports
• Lead or participate in internal, supplier, and regulatory agency audits
• Interface with FDA, notified bodies, and international regulatory authorities on compliance matters
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives to reduce defects, improve yield, and strengthen quality culture

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device environment under ISO 13485 or FDA QSR
• Working knowledge of CAPA, change control, and complaint handling processes
• Familiarity with design controls (21 CFR Part 820.30) and associated documentation
• Strong written communication skills for authoring technical documents and regulatory submissions
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Life Sciences, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• ASQ certification (CQE, CQA, or CQPA)
• Experience with MDD/MDR or IVDR regulatory frameworks
• Proficiency with electronic QMS platforms (Veeva Vault, Greenlight Guru, MasterControl)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Quality & Regulatory professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $85,000–$113,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Verification & Validation Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

• Experience with MDD/MDR or IVDR regulatory frameworks
• Proficiency with electronic QMS platforms (Veeva Vault, Greenlight Guru, MasterControl)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}

• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Quality & Regulatory professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Senior Regulatory Affairs Specialist role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Regulatory Affairs Manager
CATEGORY: Quality & Regulatory
AVG SALARY: $140,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Regulatory Affairs Manager to join our Quality & Regulatory team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Maintain and improve quality management system (QMS) processes in accordance with ISO 13485, 21 CFR Part 820, and applicable international standards
• Author, review, and approve quality documentation including SOPs, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate nonconformances, customer complaints, and CAPAs using structured root cause analysis methodologies (5-Why, fishbone, fault tree)
• Support regulatory submissions including 510(k)s, CE technical files, and post-market surveillance reports
• Lead or participate in internal, supplier, and regulatory agency audits
• Interface with FDA, notified bodies, and international regulatory authorities on compliance matters
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives to reduce defects, improve yield, and strengthen quality culture

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device environment under ISO 13485 or FDA QSR
• Working knowledge of CAPA, change control, and complaint handling processes
• Familiarity with design controls (21 CFR Part 820.30) and associated documentation
• Strong written communication skills for authoring technical documents and regulatory submissions
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Life Sciences, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

CATEGORY: Quality & Regulatory
AVG SALARY: $130,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Regulatory Affairs Consultant to join our Quality & Regulatory team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Maintain and improve quality management system (QMS) processes in accordance with ISO 13485, 21 CFR Part 820, and applicable international standards
• Author, review, and approve quality documentation including SOPs, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate nonconformances, customer complaints, and CAPAs using structured root cause analysis methodologies (5-Why, fishbone, fault tree)
• Support regulatory submissions including 510(k)s, CE technical files, and post-market surveillance reports
• Lead or participate in internal, supplier, and regulatory agency audits
• Interface with FDA, notified bodies, and international regulatory authorities on compliance matters
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives to reduce defects, improve yield, and strengthen quality culture

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device environment under ISO 13485 or FDA QSR
• Working knowledge of CAPA, change control, and complaint handling processes
• Familiarity with design controls (21 CFR Part 820.30) and associated documentation
• Strong written communication skills for authoring technical documents and regulatory submissions
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Life Sciences, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• ASQ certification (CQE, CQA, or CQPA)
• Experience with MDD/MDR or IVDR regulatory frameworks
• Proficiency with electronic QMS platforms (Veeva Vault, Greenlight Guru, MasterControl)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Quality & Regulatory professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $110,000–$155,000 base
• Target Bonus: Project-based
• Equity: Typically none
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Regulatory Affairs Consultant role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

• ASQ certification (CQE, CQA, or CQPA)
• Experience with MDD/MDR or IVDR regulatory frameworks
• Proficiency with electronic QMS platforms (Veeva Vault, Greenlight Guru, MasterControl)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Quality & Regulatory professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Post-Market Surveillance Specialist role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Manufacturing Engineer
CATEGORY: Manufacturing & Operations
AVG SALARY: $88,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Manufacturing Engineer to join our Manufacturing & Operations team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, implement, and optimize manufacturing processes for medical device production under GMP requirements
• Author and maintain manufacturing documentation including batch records, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate and resolve production nonconformances using structured root cause analysis
• Lead or support process validation activities (IQ/OQ/PQ) for equipment and manufacturing processes
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives using lean, Six Sigma, and kaizen methodologies
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and supply chain teams on NPI and product transfer activities
• Ensure production metrics (yield, cycle time, OEE) meet or exceed established targets

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device or pharmaceutical manufacturing environment
• Knowledge of FDA QSR (21 CFR Part 820), ISO 13485, and GMP requirements
• Hands-on experience with process validation and production documentation
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Operations, or related field (or equivalent experience)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Lean manufacturing certification or demonstrated kaizen leadership experience

ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Industrial Engineer to join our Manufacturing & Operations team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, implement, and optimize manufacturing processes for medical device production under GMP requirements
• Author and maintain manufacturing documentation including batch records, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate and resolve production nonconformances using structured root cause analysis
• Lead or support process validation activities (IQ/OQ/PQ) for equipment and manufacturing processes
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives using lean, Six Sigma, and kaizen methodologies
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and supply chain teams on NPI and product transfer activities
• Ensure production metrics (yield, cycle time, OEE) meet or exceed established targets

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device or pharmaceutical manufacturing environment
• Knowledge of FDA QSR (21 CFR Part 820), ISO 13485, and GMP requirements
• Hands-on experience with process validation and production documentation
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Operations, or related field (or equivalent experience)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Six Sigma Green Belt or Black Belt certification
• Experience with ERP systems (SAP, Oracle) in a manufacturing context
• Lean manufacturing certification or demonstrated kaizen leadership experience

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Manufacturing & Operations professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $72,000–$99,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–8% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Industrial Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Manufacturing & Operations professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $103,000–$138,000 base
• Target Bonus: 10–15% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Manufacturing Operations Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Director of Manufacturing
CATEGORY: Manufacturing & Operations
AVG SALARY: $165,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Director of Manufacturing to join our Manufacturing & Operations team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, implement, and optimize manufacturing processes for medical device production under GMP requirements
• Author and maintain manufacturing documentation including batch records, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate and resolve production nonconformances using structured root cause analysis
• Lead or support process validation activities (IQ/OQ/PQ) for equipment and manufacturing processes
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives using lean, Six Sigma, and kaizen methodologies
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and supply chain teams on NPI and product transfer activities
• Ensure production metrics (yield, cycle time, OEE) meet or exceed established targets

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device or pharmaceutical manufacturing environment
• Knowledge of FDA QSR (21 CFR Part 820), ISO 13485, and GMP requirements
• Hands-on experience with process validation and production documentation
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Operations, or related field (or equivalent experience)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Six Sigma Green Belt or Black Belt certification
• Experience with ERP systems (SAP, Oracle) in a manufacturing context
• Lean manufacturing certification or demonstrated kaizen leadership experience

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Manufacturing & Operations professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $142,000–$190,000 base
• Target Bonus: 15–25% of base
• Equity: Significant equity package
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Supply Chain Manager to join our Manufacturing & Operations team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, implement, and optimize manufacturing processes for medical device production under GMP requirements
• Author and maintain manufacturing documentation including batch records, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate and resolve production nonconformances using structured root cause analysis
• Lead or support process validation activities (IQ/OQ/PQ) for equipment and manufacturing processes
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives using lean, Six Sigma, and kaizen methodologies
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and supply chain teams on NPI and product transfer activities
• Ensure production metrics (yield, cycle time, OEE) meet or exceed established targets

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device or pharmaceutical manufacturing environment
• Knowledge of FDA QSR (21 CFR Part 820), ISO 13485, and GMP requirements
• Hands-on experience with process validation and production documentation
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Operations, or related field (or equivalent experience)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Six Sigma Green Belt or Black Belt certification
• Experience with ERP systems (SAP, Oracle) in a manufacturing context
• Lean manufacturing certification or demonstrated kaizen leadership experience

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Manufacturing & Operations professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $90,000–$121,000 base
• Target Bonus: 8–12% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Supply Chain Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $77,000–$104,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Supplier Quality Engineer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Production Planner
CATEGORY: Manufacturing & Operations
AVG SALARY: $65,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Production Planner to join our Manufacturing & Operations team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, implement, and optimize manufacturing processes for medical device production under GMP requirements
• Author and maintain manufacturing documentation including batch records, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate and resolve production nonconformances using structured root cause analysis
• Lead or support process validation activities (IQ/OQ/PQ) for equipment and manufacturing processes
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives using lean, Six Sigma, and kaizen methodologies
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and supply chain teams on NPI and product transfer activities
• Ensure production metrics (yield, cycle time, OEE) meet or exceed established targets

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device or pharmaceutical manufacturing environment
• Knowledge of FDA QSR (21 CFR Part 820), ISO 13485, and GMP requirements
• Hands-on experience with process validation and production documentation
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Operations, or related field (or equivalent experience)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Six Sigma Green Belt or Black Belt certification
• Experience with ERP systems (SAP, Oracle) in a manufacturing context
• Lean manufacturing certification or demonstrated kaizen leadership experience

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Design, implement, and optimize manufacturing processes for medical device production under GMP requirements
• Author and maintain manufacturing documentation including batch records, work instructions, and validation protocols
• Investigate and resolve production nonconformances using structured root cause analysis
• Lead or support process validation activities (IQ/OQ/PQ) for equipment and manufacturing processes
• Drive continuous improvement initiatives using lean, Six Sigma, and kaizen methodologies
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and supply chain teams on NPI and product transfer activities
• Ensure production metrics (yield, cycle time, OEE) meet or exceed established targets

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience in a regulated medical device or pharmaceutical manufacturing environment
• Knowledge of FDA QSR (21 CFR Part 820), ISO 13485, and GMP requirements
• Hands-on experience with process validation and production documentation
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Operations, or related field (or equivalent experience)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Six Sigma Green Belt or Black Belt certification
• Experience with ERP systems (SAP, Oracle) in a manufacturing context
• Lean manufacturing certification or demonstrated kaizen leadership experience

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Manufacturing & Operations professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $75,000–$102,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: RSUs at some companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Lean Manufacturing Specialist role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?
