• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Production Assembler role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Program Manager
CATEGORY: Program & Project Management
AVG SALARY: $130,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Program Manager to join our Program & Project Management team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Lead cross-functional program teams through medical device development programs from concept through commercialization
• Develop and maintain integrated project schedules, risk registers, and resource plans
• Facilitate stage-gate reviews and design control milestones per ISO 13485 and FDA QSR requirements
• Identify, communicate, and mitigate program risks and issues with appropriate urgency
• Provide regular program status updates to senior leadership and steering committees
• Drive accountability across engineering, quality, regulatory, clinical, and commercial workstreams
• Support design transfer activities and NPI coordination with manufacturing operations

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of program or project management experience in medical devices or regulated industry
• Understanding of medical device design controls and FDA/ISO regulatory requirements
• Proficiency with project management tools (MS Project, Smartsheet, or equivalent)
• PMP certification or equivalent project management training
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Sciences, or Business

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Develop and maintain integrated project schedules, risk registers, and resource plans
• Facilitate stage-gate reviews and design control milestones per ISO 13485 and FDA QSR requirements
• Identify, communicate, and mitigate program risks and issues with appropriate urgency
• Provide regular program status updates to senior leadership and steering committees
• Drive accountability across engineering, quality, regulatory, clinical, and commercial workstreams
• Support design transfer activities and NPI coordination with manufacturing operations

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of program or project management experience in medical devices or regulated industry
• Understanding of medical device design controls and FDA/ISO regulatory requirements
• Proficiency with project management tools (MS Project, Smartsheet, or equivalent)
• PMP certification or equivalent project management training
• Bachelor's degree in Engineering, Sciences, or Business

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Experience managing NPI or design transfer programs
• Background in engineering, quality, or regulatory affairs
• Agile or hybrid project management experience

WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Program & Project Management professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $130,000–$172,000 base
• Target Bonus: 12–18% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Senior Program Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this New Product Introduction (NPI) Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Product Manager
CATEGORY: Marketing & Product Management
AVG SALARY: $120,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Product Manager to join our Marketing & Product Management team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Define and execute product strategy, roadmap, and go-to-market plans for assigned device portfolio
• Gather voice-of-customer insights through market research, KOL advisory boards, and field feedback
• Develop compelling marketing materials, clinical messaging, and competitive positioning content
• Support product launches by coordinating with sales, clinical, regulatory, and operations teams
• Analyze market data, competitive landscape, and reimbursement environment to inform business decisions
• Manage product lifecycle including pricing, portfolio rationalization, and feature prioritization
• Measure and report on commercial performance metrics including adoption, market share, and revenue contribution

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of product management or marketing experience in medical devices or healthcare
• Strong analytical skills and comfort with market data, financial models, and competitive analysis
• Excellent communication and presentation skills — able to present to executive leadership
• Experience working cross-functionally with sales, clinical, regulatory, and engineering teams
• Bachelor's degree required; MBA preferred

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Field sales experience in medical devices
• Experience with product launches in regulated device categories
• Familiarity with reimbursement and health economics frameworks

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of product management or marketing experience in medical devices or healthcare
• Strong analytical skills and comfort with market data, financial models, and competitive analysis
• Excellent communication and presentation skills — able to present to executive leadership
• Experience working cross-functionally with sales, clinical, regulatory, and engineering teams
• Bachelor's degree required; MBA preferred

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Field sales experience in medical devices
• Experience with product launches in regulated device categories
• Familiarity with reimbursement and health economics frameworks

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Marketing & Product Management professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $155,000–$207,000 base
• Target Bonus: 15–25% of base
• Equity: Significant equity package
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Director of Product Management role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Marketing Manager
CATEGORY: Marketing & Product Management
AVG SALARY: $115,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Marketing Manager to join our Marketing & Product Management team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Define and execute product strategy, roadmap, and go-to-market plans for assigned device portfolio
• Gather voice-of-customer insights through market research, KOL advisory boards, and field feedback
• Develop compelling marketing materials, clinical messaging, and competitive positioning content
• Support product launches by coordinating with sales, clinical, regulatory, and operations teams
• Analyze market data, competitive landscape, and reimbursement environment to inform business decisions
• Manage product lifecycle including pricing, portfolio rationalization, and feature prioritization
• Measure and report on commercial performance metrics including adoption, market share, and revenue contribution

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of product management or marketing experience in medical devices or healthcare
• Strong analytical skills and comfort with market data, financial models, and competitive analysis
• Excellent communication and presentation skills — able to present to executive leadership
• Experience working cross-functionally with sales, clinical, regulatory, and engineering teams
• Bachelor's degree required; MBA preferred

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

TITLE: Global Product Marketing Manager
CATEGORY: Marketing & Product Management
AVG SALARY: $140,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Global Product Marketing Manager to join our Marketing & Product Management team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Define and execute product strategy, roadmap, and go-to-market plans for assigned device portfolio
• Gather voice-of-customer insights through market research, KOL advisory boards, and field feedback
• Develop compelling marketing materials, clinical messaging, and competitive positioning content
• Support product launches by coordinating with sales, clinical, regulatory, and operations teams
• Analyze market data, competitive landscape, and reimbursement environment to inform business decisions
• Manage product lifecycle including pricing, portfolio rationalization, and feature prioritization
• Measure and report on commercial performance metrics including adoption, market share, and revenue contribution

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of product management or marketing experience in medical devices or healthcare
• Strong analytical skills and comfort with market data, financial models, and competitive analysis
• Excellent communication and presentation skills — able to present to executive leadership
• Experience working cross-functionally with sales, clinical, regulatory, and engineering teams
• Bachelor's degree required; MBA preferred

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Field sales experience in medical devices
• Experience with product launches in regulated device categories
• Familiarity with reimbursement and health economics frameworks

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

• Author technical reports, study protocols, scientific manuscripts, and regulatory submission documents
• Maintain rigorous experimental documentation in accordance with GLP or research quality standards
• Collaborate with cross-functional teams including R&D engineering, clinical affairs, and regulatory
• Present research findings to internal leadership, external collaborators, and at scientific conferences
• Contribute to intellectual property strategy through invention disclosures and patent filings
• Stay current with scientific literature and competitive intelligence in relevant research domains

• Publication record in peer-reviewed journals
• Experience with regulatory submissions incorporating preclinical or clinical data
• Prior industry experience in a medical device, biotech, or pharmaceutical environment

WHY JOIN {{company_name}}

• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Scientific & Research professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Research Scientist role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Senior Research Scientist
CATEGORY: Scientific & Research
AVG SALARY: $135,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Senior Research Scientist to join our Scientific & Research team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Design and conduct scientific experiments to investigate new materials, technologies, or clinical solutions
• Author technical reports, study protocols, scientific manuscripts, and regulatory submission documents
• Maintain rigorous experimental documentation in accordance with GLP or research quality standards
• Collaborate with cross-functional teams including R&D engineering, clinical affairs, and regulatory
• Present research findings to internal leadership, external collaborators, and at scientific conferences
• Contribute to intellectual property strategy through invention disclosures and patent filings
• Stay current with scientific literature and competitive intelligence in relevant research domains

Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Clinical Biostatistician
CATEGORY: Scientific & Research
AVG SALARY: $130,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Clinical Biostatistician to join our Scientific & Research team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES

• Design and conduct scientific experiments to investigate new materials, technologies, or clinical solutions
• Author technical reports, study protocols, scientific manuscripts, and regulatory submission documents
• Maintain rigorous experimental documentation in accordance with GLP or research quality standards
• Collaborate with cross-functional teams including R&D engineering, clinical affairs, and regulatory
• Present research findings to internal leadership, external collaborators, and at scientific conferences
• Contribute to intellectual property strategy through invention disclosures and patent filings
• Stay current with scientific literature and competitive intelligence in relevant research domains

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Advanced degree (MS or PhD) in biology, chemistry, materials science, biomedical engineering, or related field
• Research experience in an industry, academic, or clinical setting
• Strong scientific writing and data analysis skills
• Ability to work independently and manage multiple research initiatives simultaneously

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Scientific & Research professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Medical Writer role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Talent Acquisition Specialist to join our Human Resources & Talent team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

• Manage full-cycle recruiting for technical, commercial, and operational roles within the medical device industry
• Design and administer HR programs including performance management, compensation benchmarking, and learning initiatives
• Provide HR advisory support to managers on employee relations, organizational design, and workforce planning
• Ensure compliance with applicable employment laws, EEOC regulations, and company policy
• Analyze HR metrics and provide data-driven insights to support business decisions
• Lead onboarding, training, and engagement programs that support retention and culture goals

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Working knowledge of employment law, EEOC compliance, and HR best practices

ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing HR Business Partner to join our Human Resources & Talent team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Partner with business leaders to identify workforce needs and execute talent acquisition and development strategies
• Manage full-cycle recruiting for technical, commercial, and operational roles within the medical device industry
• Design and administer HR programs including performance management, compensation benchmarking, and learning initiatives
• Provide HR advisory support to managers on employee relations, organizational design, and workforce planning
• Ensure compliance with applicable employment laws, EEOC regulations, and company policy
• Analyze HR metrics and provide data-driven insights to support business decisions
• Lead onboarding, training, and engagement programs that support retention and culture goals

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of HR experience, ideally within a medical device, biotech, or regulated industry
• Working knowledge of employment law, EEOC compliance, and HR best practices
• Experience with HRIS systems (Workday, ADP, SuccessFactors)
• Strong interpersonal and communication skills; ability to navigate sensitive situations professionally
• Bachelor's degree in HR, Business, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• PHR, SPHR, or SHRM-CP/SCP certification
• Experience supporting a manufacturing or R&D workforce
• Familiarity with GMP training requirements in a regulated environment

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Human Resources & Talent professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $85,000–$116,000 base
• Target Bonus: 8–12% of base
• Equity: RSUs at public companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this HR Business Partner role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Human Resources & Talent professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Learning & Development Manager role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: Finance Manager – Medical Device
CATEGORY: Finance & Strategy
AVG SALARY: $110,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Finance Manager – Medical Device to join our Finance & Strategy team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES

• Lead financial planning, budgeting, and forecasting processes for assigned business unit or corporate function
• Prepare and present monthly financial reporting packages including variance analysis and management commentary
• Partner with commercial, operations, and R&D leadership on strategic planning and resource allocation decisions
• Build and maintain financial models to support business cases, pricing analysis, and investment decisions
• Ensure compliance with accounting policies, internal controls, and Sarbanes-Oxley requirements
• Manage relationships with external auditors, tax advisors, and financial institutions as appropriate
• Provide ad hoc analytical support for M&A, partnership, and strategic initiative evaluations

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

• 3+ years of financial analysis, FP&A, or corporate finance experience in a medical device or healthcare company
• Advanced Excel and financial modeling proficiency
• Strong business partnering and communication skills
• Understanding of GAAP accounting, revenue recognition, and cost structures in manufacturing or commercial environments
• Bachelor's degree in Finance, Accounting, or Business; CPA or MBA preferred

ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing Pricing Analyst to join our Finance & Strategy team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Lead financial planning, budgeting, and forecasting processes for assigned business unit or corporate function
• Prepare and present monthly financial reporting packages including variance analysis and management commentary
• Partner with commercial, operations, and R&D leadership on strategic planning and resource allocation decisions
• Build and maintain financial models to support business cases, pricing analysis, and investment decisions
• Ensure compliance with accounting policies, internal controls, and Sarbanes-Oxley requirements
• Manage relationships with external auditors, tax advisors, and financial institutions as appropriate
• Provide ad hoc analytical support for M&A, partnership, and strategic initiative evaluations

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of financial analysis, FP&A, or corporate finance experience in a medical device or healthcare company
• Advanced Excel and financial modeling proficiency
• Strong business partnering and communication skills
• Understanding of GAAP accounting, revenue recognition, and cost structures in manufacturing or commercial environments
• Bachelor's degree in Finance, Accounting, or Business; CPA or MBA preferred

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience with ERP systems (SAP, Oracle) and BI tools (Tableau, Power BI)
• Medical device industry experience including familiarity with reimbursement and commercial operations
• M&A or strategic finance project experience

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHY JOIN {{company_name}}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Finance & Strategy professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
COMPENSATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Base Salary: $72,000–$99,000 base
• Target Bonus: 5–10% of base
• Equity: RSUs at some companies
• Benefits: Medical, dental, vision, 401(k) with company match, HSA/FSA, paid parental leave, professional development budget
• Note: Actual compensation varies by experience, geography, and company stage

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
INTERVIEW PROCESS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Recruiter screen (30 min) — background, compensation alignment, and motivation
2. Hiring manager interview (60 min) — functional depth, domain experience, and problem-solving
3. Cross-functional panel interview — team fit, collaboration style, and role-specific case discussion
4. Reference checks (2–3 professional references from direct managers or cross-functional partners)
5. Offer and onboarding discussion

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AI SCREENING QUESTIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
Q1: Walk me through your most relevant experience for this Pricing Analyst role.
Q2: What drew you to the medical device industry and what keeps you here?
Q3: Describe the most technically or operationally complex challenge you've solved in your current role.
Q4: How do you stay current on regulatory, clinical, or technical developments in your field?
Q5: Tell me about a time you had to influence a decision without having direct authority.
Q6: How do you manage competing priorities when multiple high-urgency items land simultaneously?
Q7: Describe a time you had to deliver difficult news to a stakeholder. How did you handle it?
Q8: What does your ideal manager do that brings out your best work?
Q9: Where are you in your career and what does the next step look like to you?
Q10: What would your current manager say is your greatest strength and your biggest development area?

TITLE: IT Systems Analyst – Medical Devices
CATEGORY: Information Technology
AVG SALARY: $90,000

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
ABOUT THE COMPANY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{{company_name}} is {{company_description}}. The company develops, manufactures, and commercializes {{product}} with a commitment to improving patient outcomes and advancing the standard of care. With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
POSITION OVERVIEW
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
{company_name} is seeking a high-performing IT Systems Analyst – Medical Devices to join our Information Technology team. In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
KEY RESPONSIBILITIES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Support, develop, or secure technology systems used in medical device development, manufacturing, or commercial operations
• Ensure technology implementations comply with FDA 21 CFR Part 11, IEC 62304, and applicable cybersecurity guidance
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and operations teams on system validation and qualification activities
• Develop technical documentation including system specifications, validation protocols, and risk assessments
• Manage vendor relationships and software lifecycles for enterprise and operational technology systems
• Monitor system performance, security posture, and compliance status across the IT portfolio
• Support incident response, patch management, and business continuity planning activities

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
REQUIRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• 3+ years of IT, software engineering, or cybersecurity experience in a regulated industry
• Understanding of FDA computer system validation (CSV) or software lifecycle (IEC 62304) requirements
• Strong analytical and problem-solving skills
• Bachelor's degree in Computer Science, Information Systems, or related field

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
• Experience with medical device software or connected health platforms
• Cybersecurity certifications (CISSP, CISM, CEH) for security-focused roles
• Familiarity with NIST Cybersecurity Framework and FDA premarket cybersecurity guidance

• Join a team building technology that meaningfully improves patient outcomes
• Competitive compensation at the top of the market for Information Technology professionals
• High-growth environment with clear pathways for advancement and expanded scope
• Collaborative culture that values technical excellence, cross-functional partnership, and personal development

With a culture built on scientific rigor, regulatory excellence, and commercial execution, {{company_name}} offers experienced professionals the opportunity to do meaningful work in a high-growth environment.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

In this role, you will bring deep domain expertise, cross-functional collaboration skills, and a commitment to quality and compliance that defines the medical device industry. This is an opportunity to contribute to meaningful work at a company that takes innovation, patient safety, and commercial excellence seriously.

• Ensure technology implementations comply with FDA 21 CFR Part 11, IEC 62304, and applicable cybersecurity guidance
• Collaborate with quality, engineering, and operations teams on system validation and qualification activities
• Develop technical documentation including system specifications, validation protocols, and risk assessments
• Manage vendor relationships and software lifecycles for enterprise and operational technology systems
• Monitor system performance, security posture, and compliance status across the IT portfolio
• Support incident response, patch management, and business continuity planning activities

================================================================================
AI ENGINE 1: JOB DESCRIPTION GENERATOR PROMPT
================================================================================

SYSTEM: You are a senior medical device recruiter and hiring strategist with 20 years of experience across Quality, R&D, Sales, Clinical, and Operations functions. You write job descriptions that attract top-quartile candidates — not job postings that read like compliance documents.

USER PROMPT:
Generate a complete, elite-quality medical device job description using the following inputs:

JOB TITLE: [Insert title]
INDUSTRY SEGMENT: [Insert — e.g., orthopedics, cardiovascular, diagnostics, neuro, capital equipment]
COMPANY TYPE: [Insert — e.g., large public OEM, high-growth startup, CRO, contract manufacturer, CDMO]
HEADCOUNT: [Insert — individual contributor / manager / director / VP]
KEY FOCUS AREAS: [Insert 2–3 things that matter most for this hire]
COMPENSATION RANGE: [Insert base + bonus + equity if applicable]

OUTPUT REQUIREMENTS:
• About the Company: 3–4 sentences using {{company_name}}, {{company_description}}, {{product}} placeholders
• Position Overview: 3–5 sentences — compelling, specific, no filler
• Key Responsibilities: 6–8 bullets — action verbs, specific, no passive language
• Required Qualifications: 5–6 bullets — true must-haves only
• Preferred Qualifications: 3–4 bullets — differentiators, not requirements in disguise
• Why Join: 4 bullets — Impact, Growth, Product, Culture
• Compensation: Base range, bonus target, equity, benefits note
• Interview Process: 4–5 structured steps
• AI Screening Questions: 8–10 role-specific behavioral and situational questions

TONE RULES:
• Write for the candidate, not HR
• No "we are looking for" or "the ideal candidate will"
• Be specific — generic language disqualifies your posting
• Every responsibility must be something the person will actually do on day one
• Every requirement must be something you would actually reject someone for not having

================================================================================
AI ENGINE 2: RESUME REWRITE ENGINE
================================================================================

SYSTEM: You are an elite resume strategist and executive recruiter who has placed hundreds of medical device professionals at companies including Medtronic, Abbott, Stryker, BD, Edwards, and high-growth startups. You rewrite resumes to reflect the candidate's actual impact — not just their job duties.

USER PROMPT:
Rewrite this resume to match the following target role. The output must make this candidate sound like a top 1% applicant — not through exaggeration, but through precise positioning of real experience.

TARGET ROLE: [Insert job title and company type]
TARGET JD: [Paste the job description or key requirements]
CANDIDATE RESUME: [Paste existing resume text]

REWRITE RULES:
1. Lead with a 3-sentence executive summary that directly mirrors the JD's top 2–3 requirements
2. Reframe every bullet to start with a strong action verb followed by context, action, and result
3. Quantify everything possible — add "approximately" or estimated ranges if exact numbers aren't provided
4. Remove all responsibilities that don't map to the target role
5. Add regulatory, clinical, or technical keywords from the JD naturally into relevant bullets
6. Reorder work history to lead with the most relevant experience for this specific role
7. Ensure the resume passes an ATS scan for the target role's top 10 keywords
8. Flag any gap in the candidate's background that needs to be addressed proactively in a cover letter

OUTPUT FORMAT:
• [Candidate Name]
• Executive Summary (3 sentences max)
• Core Competencies (8–10 keywords, comma-separated)
• Work Experience (reverse chronological, 3–5 bullets per role)
• Education
• Certifications & Professional Affiliations
• Flag: [Any gaps or weaknesses to address in cover letter or phone screen]

================================================================================
AI ENGINE 3: INTERVIEW QUESTION ENGINE
================================================================================

SYSTEM: You are a world-class talent assessment specialist and organizational psychologist who designs structured interview processes for regulated medical device companies. You create questions that predict on-the-job performance, not just interview performance.

USER PROMPT:
Generate a complete structured interview guide for the following role:

JOB TITLE: [Insert]
SENIORITY: [IC / Manager / Director / VP]
CATEGORY: [Quality & Regulatory / Sales / Engineering / Clinical / Manufacturing / etc.]
TOP 3 COMPETENCIES TO ASSESS: [Insert — e.g., regulatory strategy, territory development, design controls]

OUTPUT FORMAT:

SECTION 1: TECHNICAL / DOMAIN QUESTIONS (5 questions)
Questions that assess functional depth specific to this role. Include expected answer benchmarks.

SECTION 2: BEHAVIORAL QUESTIONS — STAR FORMAT (5 questions)
Questions that surface past behavior as a predictor of future performance. Each must specify what competency it assesses.

SECTION 3: SITUATIONAL / CASE QUESTIONS (3 questions)
Present realistic scenarios this person will face. Assess decision-making quality, not just knowledge.

SECTION 4: CULTURE & MOTIVATION QUESTIONS (3 questions)
Assess alignment to company stage, environment, and growth expectations.

SECTION 5: RED FLAGS TO WATCH FOR
List 5–7 specific red flags for this role — answers or patterns that signal a candidate is not ready or is a flight risk.

SECTION 6: SCORING RUBRIC
For each competency assessed, provide a 1–4 scoring guide:
1 = Significant gap — does not meet bar
2 = Developing — could grow into role with support
3 = Solid — meets the bar, ready to contribute now
4 = Exceptional — exceeds bar, raises team capability

================================================================================
AI ENGINE 4A: CANDIDATE OUTREACH MESSAGE
================================================================================

SYSTEM: You are Jonah Adelman, a senior medical device recruiter at The Staffing Specialist. You have 25 years of recruiting experience. Your outreach is known for being direct, human, and never sounding like a form email.

USER PROMPT:
Write a cold outreach message to a passive candidate for the following role. It must feel like it was written specifically for this person — not broadcast to 500 people.

CANDIDATE NAME: [First name]
CANDIDATE TITLE/BACKGROUND: [What you know about them]
TARGET ROLE: [Job title and brief description]
COMPANY: [If disclosed] OR [Confidential search]
HOOK: [What specifically about their background made you reach out]
PLATFORM: [LinkedIn InMail / Email / Text]

OUTPUT RULES:
• LinkedIn: 3 short paragraphs, under 300 words, no bullet points
• Email: Subject line + 3 paragraphs, under 400 words
• Text: Under 160 characters for first message, conversational
• First sentence must not start with "I" or "My name is"
• Reference one specific thing from their background
• End with a single, low-friction call to action
• No attachments, no JD links in the first message
• Sound like a human, not a recruiter

================================================================================
AI ENGINE 4B: HIRING MANAGER SUBMISSION EMAIL
================================================================================

SYSTEM: You are a seasoned medical device recruiter presenting a candidate to a hiring manager. Your submissions are known for being concise, compelling, and making it easy for the hiring manager to say yes.

USER PROMPT:
Write a candidate submission email to a hiring manager for the following situation:

CANDIDATE NAME: [Full name]
TARGET ROLE: [Title and department]
HIRING MANAGER: [Name and title]
COMPANY: [Company name]
TOP 3 REASONS THIS CANDIDATE: [List the 3 strongest fit factors]
CANDIDATE'S CURRENT SITUATION: [Current employer, title, comp, availability]
ANY CONCERNS TO ADDRESS: [Optional — flag and pre-address any gaps]

OUTPUT FORMAT:
• Subject line: Direct and specific (e.g., "Submission: [Name] — [Role]")
• Paragraph 1: Why you're excited about this candidate in 2–3 sentences
• Candidate snapshot table: Title, Company, Tenure, Compensation, Availability, Education
• Top 3 bullets: Specific qualifications mapped to the JD's top requirements
• Paragraph 2 (optional): Pre-address any concern or gap proactively
• Close: Clear ask — interview request with suggested time flexibility

================================================================================
AI ENGINE 4C: CLIENT PITCH MESSAGE
================================================================================

SYSTEM: You are Jonah Adelman at The Staffing Specialist, pitching a new search engagement to a hiring manager or HR leader at a medical device company. Your pitches are respected because they are specific, data-driven, and never waste the client's time.

USER PROMPT:
Write a cold outreach or follow-up message pitching The Staffing Specialist's recruiting services to a potential client at a medical device company. Make it specific to their situation.

CLIENT NAME: [Name and title]
COMPANY: [Company name]
WHAT YOU KNOW ABOUT THEM: [Open roles, growth stage, recent funding, news, hiring pain]
YOUR ANGLE: [What specifically makes TSS the right partner for this client]
DESIRED OUTCOME: [30-min intro call / response to email]
PLATFORM: [Email / LinkedIn / Phone voicemail script]

OUTPUT RULES:
• Email: Subject + 3 paragraphs under 350 words
• LinkedIn: 2–3 short paragraphs under 250 words
• Phone script: 30–45 second voicemail — conversational, no filler
• Reference a specific role, challenge, or detail about their company
• Lead with insight, not with a sales pitch
• Include one clear data point that establishes credibility (e.g., "placed 23 QA engineers in MedTech in 2024")
• End with a specific, easy ask
